  "default": "supervised",\n    "description": "How should Murphy execute this?"\n  },\n  "confidence_threshold": {\n    "type": "number",\n    "min": 0.0,\n    "max": 1.0,\n    "default": 0.7,\n    "description": "Minimum confidence to proceed automatically"\n  },\n  "additional_context": {\n    "type": "text",\n    "description": "Any additional information for this task?",\n    "required": false\n  }\n}\n```\n\n**Processing Flow**:\n1. **Load task specification** (from plan)\n2. **Validate prerequisites** (check dependencies completed)\n3. **Compute uncertainty scores** (UD, UA, UI, UR, UG)\n4. **Calculate confidence** (C)\n5. **Murphy Gate decision** (proceed if C > threshold)\n6. **Execute task** (through phase-based execution)\n7. **Validate output** (against acceptance criteria)\n8. **Request human review** (if needed)\n9. **Store results** (with audit trail)\n\n**Output**: Task deliverable with validation status and confidence scores\n\n---\n\n### 3.4 Validation Form\n\n**Purpose**: Human validates Murphy\'s output\n\n**Form Fields**:\n```json\n{\n  "form_type": "validation",\n  "task_id": {\n    "type": "string",\n    "required": true\n  },\n  "output_id": {\n    "type": "string",\n    "description": "ID of the output to validate",\n    "required": true\n  },\n  "validation_result": {\n    "type": "select",\n    "options": ["approved", "approved_with_changes", "rejected"],\n    "required": true\n  },\n  "quality_score": {\n    "type": "number",\n    "min": 0,\n    "max": 10,\n    "description": "Rate the quality (0-10)",\n    "required": true\n  },\n  "feedback": {\n    "type": "text",\n    "description": "What was good? What needs improvement?",\n    "required": true\n  },\n  "corrections": {\n    "type": "object",\n    "description": "Specific corrections made",\n    "required": false\n  }\n}\n```\n\n**Processing Flow**:\n1. **Load original output**\n2. **Capture validation result**\n3. **Store feedback**\n4. **If corrections made**: Capture before/after\n5. **Update task status**\n6. **Trigger shadow agent training** (if corrections exist)\n7. **Update confidence model** (based on validation)\n8. **Store in audit log**\n\n**Output**: Validation record with feedback and corrections\n\n---\n\n### 3.5 Correction Form\n\n**Purpose**: Human corrects Murphy\'s output, system learns\n\n**Form Fields**:\n```json\n{\n  "form_type": "correction",\n  "task_id": {\n    "type": "string",\n    "required": true\n  },\n  "output_id": {\n    "type": "string",\n    "required": true\n  },\n  "correction_type": {\n    "type": "select_multiple",\n    "options": [\n      "factual_error",\n      "logic_error",\n      "formatting_issue",\n      "incomplete",\n      "wrong_approach",\n      "missing_context",\n      "other"\n    ],\n    "required": true\n  },\n  "original_output": {\n    "type": "object",\n    "description": "Murphy\'s original output (auto-filled)",\n    "readonly": true\n  },\n  "corrected_output": {\n    "type": "object",\n    "description": "Your corrected version",\n    "required": true\n  },\n  "correction_rationale": {\n    "type": "text",\n    "description": "Why did you make these changes?",\n    "required": true\n  },\n  "severity": {\n    "type": "select",\n    "options": ["minor", "moderate", "major", "critical"],\n    "required": true,\n    "description": "How serious was the error?"\n  }\n}\n```\n\n**Processing Flow**:\n1. **Capture original output** (before)\n2. **Capture corrected output** (after)\n3. **Compute diff** (what changed)\n4. **Extract correction patterns** (what type of error)\n5. **Create training example**:\n   ```json\n   {\n     "input": "task context + original prompt",\n     "wrong_output": "Murphy\'s output",\n     "correct_output": "Human\'s correction",\n     "correction_type": "error category",\n     "rationale": "why it was wrong"\n   }\n   ```\n6. **Add to training dataset**\n7. **Trigger shadow agent retraining**\n8. **Update error statistics**\n9. **Store in audit log**\n\n**Output**: Training example for shadow agent\n\n---\n\n## 4. EXECUTION ENGINE ARCHITECTURE\n\n### 4.1 Phase-Based Execution (Using Existing System)\n\n**Current Implementation**: `confidence_engine/phase_controller.py`\n\n**Phases**:\n1. **EXPAND**: Generate all possibilities\n2. **TYPE**: Classify and categorize options\n3. **ENUMERATE**: List all options explicitly\n4. **CONSTRAIN**: Apply rules, limits, requirements\n5. **COLLAPSE**: Select best option(s)\n6. **BIND**: Commit to decision\n7. **EXECUTE**: Perform action\n\n**Integration with Forms**:\n```python\nclass FormDrivenExecutor:\n    """\n    Executes tasks using phase-based approach\n    """\n    \n    def __init__(self):\n        self.phase_controller = PhaseController()\n        self.confidence_engine = ConfidenceEngine()\n        self.murphy_gate = MurphyGate()\n        self.assumption_registry = AssumptionRegistry()\n        \n    def execute_task(self, task_form: TaskExecutionForm) -> TaskResult:\n        """\n        Execute task through phases with Murphy validation\n        """\n        # Load task specification\n        task = self.load_task(task_form.plan_id, task_form.task_id)\n        \n        # Initialize execution context\n        context = ExecutionContext(\n            task=task,\n            mode=task_form.execution_mode,\n            confidence_threshold=task_form.confidence_threshold\n        )\n        \n        # Execute through phases\n        for phase in [Phase.EXPAND, Phase.TYPE, Phase.ENUMERATE, \n                      Phase.CONSTRAIN, Phase.COLLAPSE, Phase.BIND, Phase.EXECUTE]:\n            \n            # Compute confidence for this phase\n            confidence = self.confidence_engine.compute_confidence(\n                phase=phase,\n                context=context\n            )\n            \n            # Murphy Gate decision\n            gate_result = self.murphy_gate.evaluate(\n                confidence=confidence,\n                threshold=task_form.confidence_threshold,\n                phase=phase\n            )\n            \n            if not gate_result.allowed:\n                # Trigger human-in-the-loop\n                return self.request_human_intervention(\n                    task=task,\n                    phase=phase,\n                    reason=gate_result.reason,\n                    confidence=confidence\n                )\n            \n            # Execute phase\n            phase_result = self.phase_controller.execute_phase(\n                phase=phase,\n                context=context\n            )\n            \n            # Update context with phase result\n            context.update(phase_result)\n            \n            # Check for assumption invalidations\n            invalidations = self.check_assumptions(context)\n            if invalidations:\n                return self.handle_invalidations(task, invalidations)\n        \n        # Task complete\n        return TaskResult(\n            task_id=task.task_id,\n            status="complete",\n            output=context.final_output,\n            confidence=confidence,\n            audit_trail=context.audit_trail\n        )\n```\n\n---\n\n### 4.2 Murphy Validation Integration\n\n**Current Implementation**: `confidence_engine/confidence_calculator.py`, `murphy_calculator.py`\n\n**Enhancement**: Add explicit UD/UA/UI/UR/UG calculations\n\n```python\nclass MurphyValidator:\n    """\n    Computes Murphy uncertainty scores and confidence\n    """\n    \n    def __init__(self):\n        self.confidence_calculator = ConfidenceCalculator()\n        self.murphy_calculator = MurphyCalculator()\n        \n    def compute_uncertainty_scores(self, task: Task, context: ExecutionContext) -> UncertaintyScores:\n        """\n        Compute all uncertainty components\n        """\n        # Data Uncertainty (UD): Quality and completeness of data\n        UD = self.compute_data_uncertainty(task, context)\n        \n        # Authority Uncertainty (UA): Credibility of sources\n        UA = self.compute_authority_uncertainty(task, context)\n        \n        # Intent Uncertainty (UI): Clarity of goals\n        UI = self.compute_intent_uncertainty(task, context)\n        \n        # Risk Uncertainty (UR): Potential consequences\n        UR = self.compute_risk_uncertainty(task, context)\n        \n        # Disagreement Uncertainty (UG): Conflicting information\n        UG = self.compute_disagreement_uncertainty(task, context)\n        \n        return UncertaintyScores(\n            UD=UD, UA=UA, UI=UI, UR=UR, UG=UG\n        )\n    \n    def compute_confidence(self, uncertainty_scores: UncertaintyScores) -> float:\n        """\n        Aggregate uncertainty scores into confidence\n        \n        Formula: C = 1 - (w_d·UD + w_a·UA + w_i·UI + w_r·UR + w_g·UG)\n        \n        Where weights sum to 1.0\n        """\n        weights = {\n            \'data\': 0.25,\n            \'authority\': 0.20,\n            \'intent\': 0.15,\n            \'risk\': 0.25,\n            \'disagreement\': 0.15\n        }\n        \n        total_uncertainty = (\n            weights[\'data\'] * uncertainty_scores.UD +\n            weights[\'authority\'] * uncertainty_scores.UA +\n            weights[\'intent\'] * uncertainty_scores.UI +\n            weights[\'risk\'] * uncertainty_scores.UR +\n            weights[\'disagreement\'] * uncertainty_scores.UG\n        )\n        \n        confidence = 1.0 - total_uncertainty\n        return max(0.0, min(1.0, confidence))\n    \n    def compute_data_uncertainty(self, task: Task, context: ExecutionContext) -> float:\n        """\n        UD: Data quality and completeness\n        \n        Factors:\n        - Completeness: % of required data available\n        - Accuracy: Verified vs unverified data\n        - Timeliness: How recent is the data\n        - Consistency: Contradictions in data\n        """\n        completeness = self._assess_completeness(task, context)\n        accuracy = self._assess_accuracy(task, context)\n        timeliness = self._assess_timeliness(task, context)\n        consistency = self._assess_consistency(task, context)\n        \n        # UD = 1 - average of quality factors\n        quality = (completeness + accuracy + timeliness + consistency) / 4\n        UD = 1.0 - quality\n        \n        return UD\n    \n    def compute_authority_uncertainty(self, task: Task, context: ExecutionContext) -> float:\n        """\n        UA: Source credibility and expertise\n        \n        Factors:\n        - Credentials: Verified expertise\n        - Reputation: Track record\n        - Consensus: Agreement among experts\n        - Bias: Potential conflicts of interest\n        """\n        credentials = self._assess_credentials(task, context)\n        reputation = self._assess_reputation(task, context)\n        consensus = self._assess_consensus(task, context)\n        bias = self._assess_bias(task, context)\n        \n        # UA = 1 - average of authority factors\n        authority = (credentials + reputation + consensus + (1 - bias)) / 4\n        UA = 1.0 - authority\n        \n        return UA\n    \n    def compute_intent_uncertainty(self, task: Task, context: ExecutionContext) -> float:\n        """\n        UI: Clarity of goals and requirements\n        \n        Factors:\n        - Specificity: How specific are requirements\n        - Measurability: Can success be measured\n        - Ambiguity: Unclear or contradictory requirements\n        - Completeness: All requirements specified\n        """\n        specificity = self._assess_specificity(task)\n        measurability = self._assess_measurability(task)\n        ambiguity = self._assess_ambiguity(task)\n        completeness = self._assess_requirement_completeness(task)\n        \n        # UI = 1 - average of clarity factors\n        clarity = (specificity + measurability + (1 - ambiguity) + completeness) / 4\n        UI = 1.0 - clarity\n        \n        return UI\n    \n    def compute_risk_uncertainty(self, task: Task, context: ExecutionContext) -> float:\n        """\n        UR: Potential negative consequences\n        \n        Factors:\n        - Impact: Severity of potential failures\n        - Probability: Likelihood of failures\n        - Reversibility: Can failures be undone\n        - Mitigation: Are mitigations in place\n        """\n        impact = self._assess_impact(task, context)\n        probability = self._assess_failure_probability(task, context)\n        reversibility = self._assess_reversibility(task)\n        mitigation = self._assess_mitigation(task, context)\n        \n        # UR = weighted average of risk factors\n        # Impact and probability weighted higher\n        UR = (\n            0.35 * impact +\n            0.35 * probability +\n            0.15 * (1 - reversibility) +\n            0.15 * (1 - mitigation)\n        )\n        \n        return UR\n    \n    def compute_disagreement_uncertainty(self, task: Task, context: ExecutionContext) -> float:\n        """\n        UG: Conflicting information or opinions\n        \n        Factors:\n        - Contradictions: Direct conflicts in data\n        - Divergence: Different approaches suggested\n        - Controversy: Disputed best practices\n        - Resolution: Can conflicts be resolved\n        """\n        contradictions = self._detect_contradictions(context)\n        divergence = self._assess_divergence(context)\n        controversy = self._assess_controversy(task)\n        resolution = self._assess_resolution_potential(context)\n        \n        # UG = average of disagreement factors\n        UG = (contradictions + divergence + controversy + (1 - resolution)) / 4\n        \n        return UG\n```\n\n---\n\n### 4.3 Murphy Gate Implementation\n\n**New Component**: Explicit gate decision mechanism\n\n```python\nclass MurphyGate:\n    """\n    Threshold-based decision mechanism\n    \n    Decides whether to proceed with execution based on confidence\n    """\n    \n    def __init__(self):\n        self.default_threshold = 0.7\n        self.phase_thresholds = {\n            Phase.EXPAND: 0.5,      # Lower threshold for exploration\n            Phase.TYPE: 0.6,\n            Phase.ENUMERATE: 0.6,\n            Phase.CONSTRAIN: 0.7,\n            Phase.COLLAPSE: 0.75,   # Higher threshold for decisions\n            Phase.BIND: 0.8,        # Very high for commitment\n            Phase.EXECUTE: 0.85     # Highest for execution\n        }\n        \n    def evaluate(self, \n                 confidence: float, \n                 threshold: Optional[float] = None,\n                 phase: Optional[Phase] = None) -> GateResult:\n        """\n        Evaluate whether to proceed\n        \n        Returns GateResult with decision and rationale\n        """\n        # Determine threshold\n        if threshold is not None:\n            effective_threshold = threshold\n        elif phase is not None:\n            effective_threshold = self.phase_thresholds.get(phase, self.default_threshold)\n        else:\n            effective_threshold = self.default_threshold\n        \n        # Gate decision\n        allowed = confidence >= effective_threshold\n        \n        # Compute margin\n        margin = confidence - effective_threshold\n        \n        # Determine action\n        if allowed:\n            if margin > 0.15:\n                action = "proceed_automatically"\n            elif margin > 0.05:\n                action = "proceed_with_monitoring"\n            else:\n                action = "proceed_with_caution"\n        else:\n            if margin > -0.05:\n                action = "request_human_review"\n            elif margin > -0.15:\n                action = "require_human_approval"\n            else:\n                action = "block_execution"\n        \n        # Generate rationale\n        rationale = self._generate_rationale(\n            confidence=confidence,\n            threshold=effective_threshold,\n            margin=margin,\n            action=action,\n            phase=phase\n        )\n        \n        return GateResult(\n            allowed=allowed,\n            confidence=confidence,\n            threshold=effective_threshold,\n            margin=margin,\n            action=action,\n            rationale=rationale,\n            timestamp=datetime.now()\n        )\n    \n    def _generate_rationale(self, \n                           confidence: float,\n                           threshold: float,\n                           margin: float,\n                           action: str,\n                           phase: Optional[Phase]) -> str:\n        """Generate human-readable rationale for gate decision"""\n        \n        phase_str = f" in {phase.value} phase" if phase else ""\n        \n        if action == "proceed_automatically":\n            return (f"Confidence {confidence:.2f} significantly exceeds threshold {threshold:.2f}"\n                   f"{phase_str}. Proceeding automatically.")\n        \n        elif action == "proceed_with_monitoring":\n            return (f"Confidence {confidence:.2f} exceeds threshold {threshold:.2f}"\n                   f"{phase_str}. Proceeding with monitoring.")\n        \n        elif action == "proceed_with_caution":\n            return (f"Confidence {confidence:.2f} barely exceeds threshold {threshold:.2f}"\n                   f"{phase_str}. Proceeding with caution.")\n        \n        elif action == "request_human_review":\n            return (f"Confidence {confidence:.2f} slightly below threshold {threshold:.2f}"\n                   f"{phase_str}. Requesting human review.")\n        \n        elif action == "require_human_approval":\n            return (f"Confidence {confidence:.2f} below threshold {threshold:.2f}"\n                   f"{phase_str}. Requiring human approval.")\n        \n        else:  # block_execution\n            return (f"Confidence {confidence:.2f} significantly below threshold {threshold:.2f}"\n                   f"{phase_str}. Execution blocked.")\n```\n\n---\n\n## 5. HUMAN-IN-THE-LOOP ARCHITECTURE\n\n### 5.1 Checkpoint System\n\n**Current Implementation**: `system_integrator.py` (triggers)\n\n**Enhancement**: Formalized checkpoint system\n\n```python\nclass HumanInTheLoopMonitor:\n    """\n    Manages human intervention checkpoints\n    """\n    \n    def __init__(self):\n        self.checkpoint_types = {\n            \'before_execution\': self._checkpoint_before_execution,\n            \'after_each_phase\': self._checkpoint_after_phase,\n            \'on_high_risk\': self._checkpoint_high_risk,\n            \'on_low_confidence\': self._checkpoint_low_confidence,\n            \'on_assumption_invalidation\': self._checkpoint_invalidation,\n            \'final_review\': self._checkpoint_final_review\n        }\n        self.pending_interventions = []\n        \n    def check_intervention_needed(self, \n                                  context: ExecutionContext,\n                                  checkpoint_config: List[str]) -> Optional[InterventionRequest]:\n        """\n        Check if human intervention is needed\n        """\n        for checkpoint_type in checkpoint_config:\n            if checkpoint_type in self.checkpoint_types:\n                checkpoint_fn = self.checkpoint_types[checkpoint_type]\n                intervention = checkpoint_fn(context)\n                \n                if intervention:\n                    return intervention\n        \n        return None\n    \n    def _checkpoint_before_execution(self, context: ExecutionContext) -> Optional[InterventionRequest]:\n        """Check before any execution"""\n        if context.phase == Phase.EXECUTE and not context.human_approved:\n            return InterventionRequest(\n                type=\'approval\',\n                reason=\'Execution requires human approval\',\n                context=context,\n                urgency=\'high\'\n            )\n        return None\n    \n    def _checkpoint_after_phase(self, context: ExecutionContext) -> Optional[InterventionRequest]:\n        """Check after each phase completion"""\n        if context.phase_completed:\n            return InterventionRequest(\n                type=\'review\',\n                reason=f\'Phase {context.phase.value} completed, review requested\',\n                context=context,\n                urgency=\'medium\'\n            )\n        return None\n    \n    def _checkpoint_high_risk(self, context: ExecutionContext) -> Optional[InterventionRequest]:\n        """Check for high-risk operations"""\n        if context.risk_score > 0.7:\n            return InterventionRequest(\n                type=\'approval\',\n                reason=f\'High risk operation detected (risk: {context.risk_score:.2f})\',\n                context=context,\n                urgency=\'high\'\n            )\n        return None\n    \n    def _checkpoint_low_confidence(self, context: ExecutionContext) -> Optional[InterventionRequest]:\n        """Check for low confidence"""\n        if context.confidence < 0.6:\n            return InterventionRequest(\n                type=\'review\',\n                reason=f\'Low confidence detected (confidence: {context.confidence:.2f})\',\n                context=context,\n                urgency=\'medium\'\n            )\n        return None\n    \n    def _checkpoint_invalidation(self, context: ExecutionContext) -> Optional[InterventionRequest]:\n        """Check for assumption invalidations"""\n        if context.invalidated_assumptions:\n            return InterventionRequest(\n                type=\'correction\',\n                reason=f\'{len(context.invalidated_assumptions)} assumptions invalidated\',\n                context=context,\n                urgency=\'high\'\n            )\n        return None\n    \n    def _checkpoint_final_review(self, context: ExecutionContext) -> Optional[InterventionRequest]:\n        """Final review before completion"""\n        if context.phase == Phase.EXECUTE and context.execution_complete:\n            return InterventionRequest(\n                type=\'validation\',\n                reason=\'Final review before marking task complete\',\n                context=context,\n                urgency=\'medium\'\n            )\n        return None\n```\n\n---\n\n## 6. CORRECTION CAPTURE AND LEARNING\n\n### 6.1 Correction Capture System\n\n**New Component**: Captures human corrections for training\n\n```python\nclass CorrectionCaptureSystem:\n    """\n    Captures human corrections and creates training examples\n    """\n    \n    def __init__(self):\n        self.training_dataset = TrainingDataset()\n        self.correction_analyzer = CorrectionAnalyzer()\n        \n    def capture_correction(self, correction_form: CorrectionForm) -> TrainingExample:\n        """\n        Capture correction and create training example\n        """\n        # Load original output\n        original = self.load_output(correction_form.output_id)\n        \n        # Compute diff\n        diff = self.compute_diff(\n            original=original.content,\n            corrected=correction_form.corrected_output\n        )\n        \n        # Analyze correction patterns\n        patterns = self.correction_analyzer.analyze(\n            original=original.content,\n            corrected=correction_form.corrected_output,\n            correction_type=correction_form.correction_type\n        )\n        \n        # Create training example\n        training_example = TrainingExample(\n            example_id=generate_id(),\n            task_type=original.task_type,\n            input_context={\n                \'task_description\': original.task.description,\n                \'requirements\': original.task.requirements,\n                \'constraints\': original.task.constraints,\n                \'phase\': original.phase\n            },\n            wrong_output=original.content,\n            correct_output=correction_form.corrected_output,\n            diff=diff,\n            correction_type=correction_form.correction_type,\n            correction_rationale=correction_form.correction_rationale,\n            severity=correction_form.severity,\n            patterns=patterns,\n            timestamp=datetime.now()\n        )\n        \n        # Add to training dataset\n        self.training_dataset.add(training_example)\n        \n        # Update error statistics\n        self.update_error_stats(training_example)\n        \n        # Store in audit log\n        self.audit_log.log_correction(training_example)\n        \n        return training_example\n    \n    def compute_diff(self, original: Any, corrected: Any) -> Dict:\n        """\n        Compute structured diff between original and corrected\n        """\n        if isinstance(original, str) and isinstance(corrected, str):\n            return self._text_diff(original, corrected)\n        elif isinstance(original, dict) and isinstance(corrected, dict):\n            return self._dict_diff(original, corrected)\n        elif isinstance(original, list) and isinstance(corrected, list):\n            return self._list_diff(original, corrected)\n        else:\n            return {\'type\': \'full_replacement\', \'original\': original, \'corrected\': corrected}\n    \n    def _text_diff(self, original: str, corrected: str) -> Dict:\n        """Compute text diff"""\n        import difflib\n        \n        diff = difflib.unified_diff(\n            original.splitlines(),\n            corrected.splitlines(),\n            lineterm=\'\'\n        )\n        \n        return {\n            \'type\': \'text\',\n            \'diff\': list(diff),\n            \'similarity\': difflib.SequenceMatcher(None, original, corrected).ratio()\n        }\n    \n    def _dict_diff(self, original: Dict, corrected: Dict) -> Dict:\n        """Compute dictionary diff"""\n        added = {k: v for k, v in corrected.items() if k not in original}\n        removed = {k: v for k, v in original.items() if k not in corrected}\n        changed = {\n            k: {\'from\': original[k], \'to\': corrected[k]}\n            for k in original.keys() & corrected.keys()\n            if original[k] != corrected[k]\n        }\n        \n        return {\n            \'type\': \'dict\',\n            \'added\': added,\n            \'removed\': removed,\n            \'changed\': changed\n        }\n    \n    def _list_diff(self, original: List, corrected: List) -> Dict:\n        """Compute list diff"""\n        added = [item for item in corrected if item not in original]\n        removed = [item for item in original if item not in corrected]\n        \n        return {\n            \'type\': \'list\',\n            \'added\': added,\n            \'removed\': removed,\n            \'original_length\': len(original),\n            \'corrected_length\': len(corrected)\n        }\n```\n\n---\n\n### 6.2 Shadow Agent Training\n\n**New Component**: Trains shadow agent from corrections\n\n```python\nclass ShadowAgentTrainer:\n    """\n    Trains shadow agent from human corrections\n    """\n    \n    def __init__(self):\n        self.training_dataset = TrainingDataset()\n        self.shadow_agent = None\n        self.primary_agent = None\n        self.performance_tracker = PerformanceTracker()\n        \n    def train_shadow_agent(self, \n                          training_examples: List[TrainingExample],\n                          validation_split: float = 0.2) -> ShadowAgent:\n        """\n        Train shadow agent on correction examples\n        """\n        # Split into training and validation\n        train_examples, val_examples = self.split_dataset(\n            training_examples,\n            validation_split\n        )\n        \n        # Initialize shadow agent\n        shadow_agent = ShadowAgent(\n            base_model=self.primary_agent.model_name,\n            training_config=self.get_training_config()\n        )\n        \n        # Train on corrections\n        training_results = shadow_agent.train(\n            training_examples=train_examples,\n            validation_examples=val_examples,\n            epochs=10,\n            batch_size=32\n        )\n        \n        # Evaluate performance\n        performance = self.evaluate_shadow_agent(\n            shadow_agent=shadow_agent,\n            validation_examples=val_examples\n        )\n        \n        # Store shadow agent\n        self.shadow_agent = shadow_agent\n        \n        # Log training results\n        self.log_training_results(training_results, performance)\n        \n        return shadow_agent\n    \n    def evaluate_shadow_agent(self,\n                             shadow_agent: ShadowAgent,\n                             validation_examples: List[TrainingExample]) -> PerformanceMetrics:\n        """\n        Evaluate shadow agent performance\n        """\n        metrics = PerformanceMetrics()\n        \n        for example in validation_examples:\n            # Get shadow agent output\n            shadow_output = shadow_agent.generate(\n                input_context=example.input_context\n            )\n            \n            # Get primary agent output (for comparison)\n            primary_output = self.primary_agent.generate(\n                input_context=example.input_context\n            )\n            \n            # Compare to correct output\n            shadow_similarity = self.compute_similarity(\n                shadow_output,\n                example.correct_output\n            )\n            \n            primary_similarity = self.compute_similarity(\n                primary_output,\n                example.correct_output\n            )\n            \n            # Track metrics\n            metrics.add_result(\n                shadow_similarity=shadow_similarity,\n                primary_similarity=primary_similarity,\n                example_type=example.task_type\n            )\n        \n        return metrics\n    \n    def ab_test(self, \n                test_cases: List[TestCase],\n                duration_days: int = 7) -> ABTestResults:\n        """\n        A/B test shadow agent vs primary agent\n        """\n        results = ABTestResults()\n        \n        for test_case in test_cases:\n            # Randomly assign to shadow or primary\n            use_shadow = random.random() < 0.5\n            \n            if use_shadow:\n                output = self.shadow_agent.generate(test_case.input_context)\n                agent_type = \'shadow\'\n            else:\n                output = self.primary_agent.generate(test_case.input_context)\n                agent_type = \'primary\'\n            \n            # Get human validation\n            validation = self.request_human_validation(\n                output=output,\n                test_case=test_case\n            )\n            \n            # Track result\n            results.add_result(\n                agent_type=agent_type,\n                validation=validation,\n                test_case=test_case\n            )\n        \n        # Analyze results\n        analysis = results.analyze()\n        \n        return analysis\n    \n    def promote_shadow_agent(self) -> bool:\n        """\n        Promote shadow agent to primary if better\n        """\n        # Get performance comparison\n        comparison = self.performance_tracker.compare_agents(\n            shadow_agent=self.shadow_agent,\n            primary_agent=self.primary_agent\n        )\n        \n        # Decision criteria\n        if (comparison.shadow_accuracy > comparison.primary_accuracy + 0.05 and\n            comparison.shadow_confidence > 0.8 and\n            comparison.sample_size > 100):\n            \n            # Promote shadow to primary\n            self.primary_agent = self.shadow_agent\n            self.shadow_agent = None\n            \n            # Log promotion\n            self.log_promotion(comparison)\n            \n            return True\n        \n        return False\n```\n\n---\n\n## 7. COST MODEL AND ROI ANALYSIS\n\n### 7.1 Cost Breakdown\n\n**Murphy System Costs** (per task):\n```\nLLM API Calls:\n- Plan generation: $0.10 - $0.50\n- Task execution: $0.20 - $2.00\n- Validation: $0.05 - $0.20\n- Correction analysis: $0.05 - $0.10\nTotal LLM: $0.40 - $2.80\n\nInfrastructure:\n- Redis/PostgreSQL: $0.01 - $0.05\n- Storage: $0.01 - $0.05\n- Compute: $0.05 - $0.20\nTotal Infrastructure: $0.07 - $0.30\n\nHuman Time (20% correction):\n- Review: 5-10 minutes @ $50-200/hr = $4.17 - $33.33\n- Correction: 10-20 minutes @ $50-200/hr = $8.33 - $66.67\nTotal Human: $12.50 - $100.00\n\nTOTAL PER TASK: $13 - $103\n```\n\n**Traditional Approach Costs** (per task):\n```\nHuman Labor:\n- Planning: 2-4 hours @ $50-200/hr = $100 - $800\n- Execution: 4-8 hours @ $50-200/hr = $200 - $1,600\n- Review: 1-2 hours @ $50-200/hr = $50 - $400\nTotal Human: $350 - $2,800\n\nTOTAL PER TASK: $350 - $2,800\n```\n\n**Cost Savings**: 90-97% reduction per task\n\n---\n\n### 7.2 ROI Calculation\n\n**Scenario**: 100-person organization, 1000 tasks/year\n\n**Traditional Approach**:\n```\nCost: 1000 tasks × $1,000 average = $1,000,000/year\nTime: 1000 tasks × 6 hours average = 6,000 hours\n```\n\n**Murphy System Approach**:\n```\nCost: 1000 tasks × $50 average = $50,000/year\nTime: 1000 tasks × 0.5 hours average (human correction) = 500 hours\n\nSavings: $950,000/year (95% reduction)\nTime Savings: 5,500 hours/year (92% reduction)\n```\n\n**Break-Even Analysis**:\n```\nMurphy System Setup Cost: $50,000 - $100,000\nAnnual Operating Cost: $50,000\nTotal Year 1 Cost: $100,000 - $150,000\n\nBreak-even: 100-150 tasks (10-15% of annual volume)\nROI Year 1: 600-900%\nROI Year 2+: 1900%+\n```\n\n---\n\n## 8. {'role': 'assistant', 'content': '<function_calls>\n<create-file file_path="murphy_implementation/validation/uncertainty_calculator.py">\n"""\nUncertainty Calculator\n\nComputes all five Murphy uncertainty components:\n- UD: Data Uncertainty\n- UA: Authority Uncertainty  \n- UI: Intent Uncertainty\n- UR: Risk Uncertainty\n- UG: Disagreement Uncertainty\n"""\n\nfrom typing import Dict, Any, List, Optional\nfrom datetime import datetime\nimport logging\n\nfrom .models import UncertaintyScores\n\nlogger = logging.getLogger(__name__)\n\n\nclass UncertaintyCalculator:\n    """\n    Calculates Murphy uncertainty scores\n    \n    All uncertainty scores are in range [0, 1] where:\n    - 0 = no uncertainty (perfect certainty)\n    - 1 = maximum uncertainty (complete uncertainty)\n    """\n    \n    def __init__(self):\n        # Weights for uncertainty components\n        self.weights = {\n            \'data\': 0.25,\n            \'authority\': 0.20,\n            \'intent\': 0.15,\n            \'risk\': 0.25,\n            \'disagreement\': 0.15\n        }\n    \n    def compute_all_uncertainties(\n        self,\n        task: Any,\n        context: Dict[str, Any]\n    ) -> UncertaintyScores:\n        """\n        Compute all uncertainty components\n        \n        Args:\n            task: Task being evaluated\n            context: Execution context with data, sources, etc.\n            \n        Returns:\n            UncertaintyScores with all components\n        """\n        UD = self.compute_data_uncertainty(task, context)\n        UA = self.compute_authority_uncertainty(task, context)\n        UI = self.compute_intent_uncertainty(task, context)\n        UR = self.compute_risk_uncertainty(task, context)\n        UG = self.compute_disagreement_uncertainty(task, context)\n        \n        return UncertaintyScores(\n            UD=UD,\n            UA=UA,\n            UI=UI,\n            UR=UR,\n            UG=UG\n        )\n    \n    def compute_data_uncertainty(\n        self,\n        task: Any,\n        context: Dict[str, Any]\n    ) -> float:\n        """\n        UD: Data quality and completeness\n        \n        Factors:\n        - Completeness: % of required data available\n        - Accuracy: Verified vs unverified data\n        - Timeliness: How recent is the data\n        - Consistency: Contradictions in data\n        \n        Returns:\n            UD score in [0, 1]\n        """\n        # Extract data quality factors\n        completeness = self._assess_completeness(task, context)\n        accuracy = self._assess_accuracy(task, context)\n        timeliness = self._assess_timeliness(task, context)\n        consistency = self._assess_consistency(task, context)\n        \n        # Average quality factors\n        quality = (completeness + accuracy + timeliness + consistency) / 4\n        \n        # UD = 1 - quality (higher quality = lower uncertainty)\n        UD = 1.0 - quality\n        \n        logger.debug(f"Data Uncertainty: UD={UD:.3f} (completeness={completeness:.2f}, accuracy={accuracy:.2f}, timeliness={timeliness:.2f}, consistency={consistency:.2f})")\n        \n        return max(0.0, min(1.0, UD))\n    \n    def compute_authority_uncertainty(\n        self,\n        task: Any,\n        context: Dict[str, Any]\n    ) -> float:\n        """\n        UA: Source credibility and expertise\n        \n        Factors:\n        - Credentials: Verified expertise\n        - Reputation: Track record\n        - Consensus: Agreement among experts\n        - Bias: Potential conflicts of interest\n        \n        Returns:\n            UA score in [0, 1]\n        """\n        # Extract authority factors\n        credentials = self._assess_credentials(task, context)\n        reputation = self._assess_reputation(task, context)\n        consensus = self._assess_consensus(task, context)\n        bias = self._assess_bias(task, context)\n        \n        # Average authority factors (bias is inverted)\n        authority = (credentials + reputation + consensus + (1 - bias)) / 4\n        \n        # UA = 1 - authority (higher authority = lower uncertainty)\n        UA = 1.0 - authority\n        \n        logger.debug(f"Authority Uncertainty: UA={UA:.3f} (credentials={credentials:.2f}, reputation={reputation:.2f}, consensus={consensus:.2f}, bias={bias:.2f})")\n        \n        return max(0.0, min(1.0, UA))\n    \n    def compute_intent_uncertainty(\n        self,\n        task: Any,\n        context: Dict[str, Any]\n    ) -> float:\n        """\n        UI: Clarity of goals and requirements\n        \n        Factors:\n        - Specificity: How specific are requirements\n        - Measurability: Can success be measured\n        - Ambiguity: Unclear or contradictory requirements\n        - Completeness: All requirements specified\n        \n        Returns:\n            UI score in [0, 1]\n        """\n        # Extract intent clarity factors\n        specificity = self._assess_specificity(task)\n        measurability = self._assess_measurability(task)\n        ambiguity = self._assess_ambiguity(task)\n        completeness = self._assess_requirement_completeness(task)\n        \n        # Average clarity factors (ambiguity is inverted)\n        clarity = (specificity + measurability + (1 - ambiguity) + completeness) / 4\n        \n        # UI = 1 - clarity (higher clarity = lower uncertainty)\n        UI = 1.0 - clarity\n        \n        logger.debug(f"Intent Uncertainty: UI={UI:.3f} (specificity={specificity:.2f}, measurability={measurability:.2f}, ambiguity={ambiguity:.2f}, completeness={completeness:.2f})")\n        \n        return max(0.0, min(1.0, UI))\n    \n    def compute_risk_uncertainty(\n        self,\n        task: Any,\n        context: Dict[str, Any]\n    ) -> float:\n        """\n        UR: Potential negative consequences\n        \n        Factors:\n        - Impact: Severity of potential failures\n        - Probability: Likelihood of failures\n        - Reversibility: Can failures be undone\n        - Mitigation: Are mitigations in place\n        \n        Returns:\n            UR score in [0, 1]\n        """\n        # Extract risk factors\n        impact = self._assess_impact(task, context)\n        probability = self._assess_failure_probability(task, context)\n        reversibility = self._assess_reversibility(task)\n        mitigation = self._assess_mitigation(task, context)\n        \n        # Weighted average (impact and probability weighted higher)\n        UR = (\n            0.35 * impact +\n            0.35 * probability +\n            0.15 * (1 - reversibility) +\n            0.15 * (1 - mitigation)\n        )\n        \n        logger.debug(f"Risk Uncertainty: UR={UR:.3f} (impact={impact:.2f}, probability={probability:.2f}, reversibility={reversibility:.2f}, mitigation={mitigation:.2f})")\n        \n        return max(0.0, min(1.0, UR))\n    \n    def compute_disagreement_uncertainty(\n        self,\n        task: Any,\n        context: Dict[str, Any]\n    ) -> float:\n        """\n        UG: Conflicting information or opinions\n        \n        Factors:\n        - Contradictions: Direct conflicts in data\n        - Divergence: Different approaches suggested\n        - Controversy: Disputed best practices\n        - Resolution: Can conflicts be resolved\n        \n        Returns:\n            UG score in [0, 1]\n        """\n        # Extract disagreement factors\n        contradictions = self._detect_contradictions(context)\n        divergence = self._assess_divergence(context)\n        controversy = self._assess_controversy(task)\n        resolution = self._assess_resolution_potential(context)\n        \n        # Average disagreement factors (resolution is inverted)\n        UG = (contradictions + divergence + controversy + (1 - resolution)) / 4\n        \n        logger.debug(f"Disagreement Uncertainty: UG={UG:.3f} (contradictions={contradictions:.2f}, divergence={divergence:.2f}, controversy={controversy:.2f}, resolution={resolution:.2f})")\n        \n        return max(0.0, min(1.0, UG))\n    \n    # ========================================================================\n    # DATA UNCERTAINTY (UD) ASSESSMENT METHODS\n    # ========================================================================\n    \n    def _assess_completeness(self, task: Any, context: Dict[str, Any]) -> float:\n        """Assess data completeness (0=incomplete, 1=complete)"""\n        # Check if all required data is available\n        required_data = context.get(\'required_data\', [])\n        available_data = context.get(\'available_data\', [])\n        \n        if not required_data:\n            return 0.8  # Default: assume mostly complete\n        \n        completeness = len(available_data) / len(required_data)\n        return min(1.0, completeness)\n    \n    def _assess_accuracy(self, task: Any, context: Dict[str, Any]) -> float:\n        """Assess data accuracy (0=unverified, 1=verified)"""\n        # Check verification status of data\n        verified_count = context.get(\'verified_data_count\', 0)\n        total_count = context.get(\'total_data_count\', 1)\n        \n        if total_count == 0:\n            return 0.5  # Default: assume partially verified\n        \n        accuracy = verified_count / total_count\n        return accuracy\n    \n    def _assess_timeliness(self, task: Any, context: Dict[str, Any]) -> float:\n        """Assess data timeliness (0=stale, 1=fresh)"""\n        # Check data freshness\n        data_age_days = context.get(\'data_age_days\', 30)\n        \n        # Exponential decay: fresh data (0 days) = 1.0, old data (90+ days) = 0.0\n        timeliness = max(0.0, 1.0 - (data_age_days / 90.0))\n        return timeliness\n    \n    def _assess_consistency(self, task: Any, context: Dict[str, Any]) -> float:\n        """Assess data consistency (0=contradictory, 1=consistent)"""\n        # Check for contradictions\n        contradiction_count = context.get(\'contradiction_count\', 0)\n        \n        if contradiction_count == 0:\n            return 1.0\n        elif contradiction_count <= 2:\n            return 0.7\n        elif contradiction_count <= 5:\n            return 0.4\n        else:\n            return 0.1\n    \n    # ========================================================================\n    # AUTHORITY UNCERTAINTY (UA) ASSESSMENT METHODS\n    # ========================================================================\n    \n    def _assess_credentials(self, task: Any, context: Dict[str, Any]) -> float:\n        """Assess source credentials (0=none, 1=verified expert)"""\n        # Check source credentials\n        source_credentials = context.get(\'source_credentials\', [])\n        \n        if not source_credentials:\n            return 0.3  # Default: assume limited credentials\n        \n        # Score based on credential quality\n        verified_experts = sum(1 for c in source_credentials if c.get(\'verified\') and c.get(\'expert\'))\n        total_sources = len(source_credentials)\n        \n        return verified_experts / total_sources if total_sources > 0 else 0.3\n    \n    def _assess_reputation(self, task: Any, context: Dict[str, Any]) -> float:\n        """Assess source reputation (0=poor, 1=excellent)"""\n        # Check source reputation scores\n        reputation_scores = context.get(\'reputation_scores\', [])\n        \n        if not reputation_scores:\n            return 0.5  # Default: assume average reputation\n        \n        avg_reputation = sum(reputation_scores) / len(reputation_scores)\n        return avg_reputation\n    \n    def _assess_consensus(self, task: Any, context: Dict[str, Any]) -> float:\n        """Assess expert consensus (0=disagreement, 1=agreement)"""\n        # Check agreement among sources\n        agreement_level = context.get(\'expert_agreement\', 0.7)\n        return agreement_level\n    \n    def _assess_bias(self, task: Any, context: Dict[str, Any]) -> float:\n        """Assess potential bias (0=unbiased, 1=highly biased)"""\n        # Check for conflicts of interest\n        bias_indicators = context.get(\'bias_indicators\', [])\n        \n        if not bias_indicators:\n            return 0.1  # Default: assume minimal bias\n        \n        # More bias indicators = higher bias score\n        bias_score = min(1.0, len(bias_indicators) * 0.2)\n        return bias_score\n    \n    # ========================================================================\n    # INTENT UNCERTAINTY (UI) ASSESSMENT METHODS\n    # ========================================================================\n    \n    def _assess_specificity(self, task: Any) -> float:\n        """Assess requirement specificity (0=vague, 1=specific)"""\n        # Check task description length and detail\n        description = getattr(task, \'description\', \'\')\n        \n        if len(description) < 50:\n            return 0.3  # Too short, likely vague\n        elif len(description) < 200:\n            return 0.6  # Moderate detail\n        else:\n            return 0.9  # Detailed description\n    \n    def _assess_measurability(self, task: Any) -> float:\n        """Assess success measurability (0=unmeasurable, 1=measurable)"""\n        # Check if validation criteria exist\n        validation_criteria = getattr(task, \'validation_criteria\', [])\n        \n        if not validation_criteria:\n            return 0.2  # No criteria = hard to measure\n        \n        # More criteria = more measurable\n        measurability = min(1.0, len(validation_criteria) * 0.3)\n        return measurability\n    \n    def _assess_ambiguity(self, task: Any) -> float:\n        """Assess requirement ambiguity (0=clear, 1=ambiguous)"""\n        # Check for ambiguous language\n        description = getattr(task, \'description\', \'\').lower()\n        \n        ambiguous_words = [\'maybe\', \'possibly\', \'might\', \'could\', \'should\', \'approximately\']\n        ambiguity_count = sum(1 for word in ambiguous_words if word in description)\n        \n        # More ambiguous words = higher ambiguity\n        ambiguity = min(1.0, ambiguity_count * 0.2)\n        return ambiguity\n    \n    def _assess_requirement_completeness(self, task: Any) -> float:\n        """Assess requirement completeness (0=incomplete, 1=complete)"""\n        # Check if key requirement aspects are specified\n        has_description = bool(getattr(task, \'description\', \'\'))\n        has_deliverables = bool(getattr(task, \'deliverables\', []))\n        has_validation = bool(getattr(task, \'validation_criteria\', []))\n        has_timeline = bool(getattr(task, \'estimated_hours\', None))\n        \n        completeness = sum([has_description, has_deliverables, has_validation, has_timeline]) / 4\n        return completeness\n    \n    # ========================================================================\n    # RISK UNCERTAINTY (UR) ASSESSMENT METHODS\n    # ========================================================================\n    \n    def _assess_impact(self, task: Any, context: Dict[str, Any]) -> float:\n        """Assess failure impact (0=minimal, 1=catastrophic)"""\n        # Check task priority and criticality\n        priority = getattr(task, \'priority\', \'medium\')\n        \n        priority_impact = {\n            \'low\': 0.2,\n            \'medium\': 0.5,\n            \'high\': 0.7,\n            \'critical\': 0.9\n        }\n        \n        return priority_impact.get(priority, 0.5)\n    \n    def _assess_failure_probability(self, task: Any, context: Dict[str, Any]) -> float:\n        """Assess failure probability (0=unlikely, 1=likely)"""\n        # Check historical failure rate and complexity\n        complexity = context.get(\'task_complexity\', \'medium\')\n        historical_failure_rate = context.get(\'historical_failure_rate\', 0.2)\n        \n        complexity_factor = {\n            \'low\': 0.1,\n            \'medium\': 0.3,\n            \'high\': 0.6,\n            \'very_high\': 0.8\n        }\n        \n        base_probability = complexity_factor.get(complexity, 0.3)\n        \n        # Adjust by historical data\n        probability = (base_probability + historical_failure_rate) / 2\n        return min(1.0, probability)\n    \n    def _assess_reversibility(self, task: Any) -> float:\n        """Assess failure reversibility (0=irreversible, 1=easily reversed)"""\n        # Check if task has rollback capability\n        risks = getattr(task, \'risks\', [])\n        \n        # Look for irreversibility indicators\n        irreversible_keywords = [\'permanent\', \'irreversible\', \'cannot undo\', \'data loss\']\n        has_irreversible = any(\n            any(keyword in risk.lower() for keyword in irreversible_keywords)\n            for risk in risks\n        )\n        \n        if has_irreversible:\n            return 0.2  # Low reversibility\n        else:\n            return 0.8  # High reversibility (default assumption)\n    \n    def _assess_mitigation(self, task: Any, context: Dict[str, Any]) -> float:\n        """Assess risk mitigation (0=no mitigation, 1=fully mitigated)"""\n        # Check if mitigations are in place\n        mitigations = context.get(\'risk_mitigations\', [])\n        risks = getattr(task, \'risks\', [])\n        \n        if not risks:\n            return 1.0  # No risks = no mitigation needed\n        \n        if not mitigations:\n            return 0.2  # Risks but no mitigations\n        \n        # Compare mitigation coverage\n        mitigation_coverage = min(1.0, len(mitigations) / len(risks))\n        return mitigation_coverage\n    \n    # ========================================================================\n    # DISAGREEMENT UNCERTAINTY (UG) ASSESSMENT METHODS\n    # ========================================================================\n    \n    def _detect_contradictions(self, context: Dict[str, Any]) -> float:\n        """Detect contradictions (0=none, 1=many)"""\n        # Check for contradictory information\n        contradiction_count = context.get(\'contradiction_count\', 0)\n        \n        if contradiction_count == 0:\n            return 0.0\n        elif contradiction_count <= 2:\n            return 0.3\n        elif contradiction_count <= 5:\n            return 0.6\n        else:\n            return 0.9\n    \n    def _assess_divergence(self, context: Dict[str, Any]) -> float:\n        """Assess approach divergence (0=consensus, 1=divergent)"""\n        # Check for different recommended approaches\n        approaches = context.get(\'recommended_approaches\', [])\n        \n        if len(approaches) <= 1:\n            return 0.0  # Single approach = no divergence\n        elif len(approaches) == 2:\n            return 0.4  # Two approaches = moderate divergence\n        else:\n            return 0.7  # Multiple approaches = high divergence\n    \n    def _assess_controversy(self, task: Any) -> float:\n        """Assess controversy level (0=accepted, 1=controversial)"""\n        # Check for controversial aspects\n        description = getattr(task, \'description\', \'\').lower()\n        \n        controversial_keywords = [\'controversial\', \'disputed\', \'debated\', \'disagreement\']\n        has_controversy = any(keyword in description for keyword in controversial_keywords)\n        \n        return 0.7 if has_controversy else 0.1\n    \n    def _assess_resolution_potential(self, context: Dict[str, Any]) -> float:\n        """Assess conflict resolution potential (0=unresolvable, 1=resolvable)"""\n        # Check if conflicts can be resolved\n        has_tiebreaker = context.get(\'has_tiebreaker\', False)\n        has_authority = context.get(\'has_decision_authority\', False)\n        \n        if has_tiebreaker and has_authority:\n            return 0.9  # High resolution potential\n        elif has_tiebreaker or has_authority:\n            return 0.6  # Moderate resolution potential\n        else:\n            return 0.3  # Low resolution potential\n</create-file>\n</function_calls>'}

{'role': 'assistant', 'content': '<function_calls>\n<create-file file_path="murphy_implementation/validation/murphy_gate.py">\n"""\nMurphy Gate\n\nThreshold-based decision mechanism that determines whether to proceed\nwith execution based on confidence scores.\n"""\n\nfrom typing import Optional\nfrom datetime import datetime\nimport logging\n\nfrom .models import GateResult, GateAction, Phase\n\nlogger = logging.getLogger(__name__)\n\n\nclass MurphyGate:\n    """\n    Murphy Gate - Threshold-based decision mechanism\n    \n    Decides whether to proceed with execution based on confidence scores.\n    Different phases have different threshold requirements.\n    """\n    \n    def __init__(self):\n        # Default threshold for all operations\n        self.default_threshold = 0.7\n        \n        # Phase-specific thresholds\n        self.phase_thresholds = {\n            Phase.EXPAND: 0.5,      # Lower threshold for exploration\n            Phase.TYPE: 0.6,        # Moderate threshold for classification\n            Phase.ENUMERATE: 0.6,   # Moderate threshold for enumeration\n            Phase.CONSTRAIN: 0.7,   # Standard threshold for constraints\n            Phase.COLLAPSE: 0.75,   # Higher threshold for decisions\n            Phase.BIND: 0.8,        # Very high for commitment\n            Phase.EXECUTE: 0.85     # Highest for execution\n        }\n        \n        # Action thresholds (margins from threshold)\n        self.action_margins = {\n            \'proceed_automatically\': 0.15,      # confidence >= threshold + 0.15\n            \'proceed_with_monitoring\': 0.05,    # confidence >= threshold + 0.05\n            \'proceed_with_caution\': 0.0,        # confidence >= threshold\n            \'request_human_review\': -0.05,      # confidence >= threshold - 0.05\n            \'require_human_approval\': -0.15,    # confidence >= threshold - 0.15\n            \'block_execution\': float(\'-inf\')    # confidence < threshold - 0.15\n        }\n    \n    def evaluate(\n        self,\n        confidence: float,\n        threshold: Optional[float] = None,\n        phase: Optional[Phase] = None,\n        context: Optional[dict] = None\n    ) -> GateResult:\n        """\n        Evaluate whether to proceed with execution\n        \n        Args:\n            confidence: Confidence score (0.0 to 1.0)\n            threshold: Custom threshold (optional, uses phase/default if not provided)\n            phase: Current execution phase (optional)\n            context: Additional context for decision (optional)\n            \n        Returns:\n            GateResult with decision and rationale\n        """\n        # Determine effective threshold\n        effective_threshold = self._determine_threshold(threshold, phase)\n        \n        # Calculate margin\n        margin = confidence - effective_threshold\n        \n        # Determine action based on margin\n        action = self._determine_action(margin)\n        \n        # Determine if allowed to proceed\n        allowed = action in [\n            GateAction.PROCEED_AUTOMATICALLY,\n            GateAction.PROCEED_WITH_MONITORING,\n            GateAction.PROCEED_WITH_CAUTION\n        ]\n        \n        # Generate rationale\n        rationale = self._generate_rationale(\n            confidence=confidence,\n            threshold=effective_threshold,\n            margin=margin,\n            action=action,\n            phase=phase\n        )\n        \n        # Create result\n        result = GateResult(\n            allowed=allowed,\n            confidence=confidence,\n            threshold=effective_threshold,\n            margin=margin,\n            action=action,\n            rationale=rationale,\n            phase=phase,\n            metadata={\n                \'context\': context or {},\n                \'decision_time\': datetime.now().isoformat()\n            }\n        )\n        \n        # Log decision\n        self._log_decision(result)\n        \n        return result\n    \n    def _determine_threshold(\n        self,\n        custom_threshold: Optional[float],\n        phase: Optional[Phase]\n    ) -> float:\n        """Determine effective threshold"""\n        if custom_threshold is not None:\n            return custom_threshold\n        elif phase is not None:\n            return self.phase_thresholds.get(phase, self.default_threshold)\n        else:\n            return self.default_threshold\n    \n    def _determine_action(self, margin: float) -> GateAction:\n        """Determine action based on margin"""\n        if margin >= self.action_margins[\'proceed_automatically\']:\n            return GateAction.PROCEED_AUTOMATICALLY\n        elif margin >= self.action_margins[\'proceed_with_monitoring\']:\n            return GateAction.PROCEED_WITH_MONITORING\n        elif margin >= self.action_margins[\'proceed_with_caution\']:\n            return GateAction.PROCEED_WITH_CAUTION\n        elif margin >= self.action_margins[\'request_human_review\']:\n            return GateAction.REQUEST_HUMAN_REVIEW\n        elif margin >= self.action_margins[\'require_human_approval\']:\n            return GateAction.REQUIRE_HUMAN_APPROVAL\n        else:\n            return GateAction.BLOCK_EXECUTION\n    \n    def _generate_rationale(\n        self,\n        confidence: float,\n        threshold: float,\n        margin: float,\n        action: GateAction,\n        phase: Optional[Phase]\n    ) -> str:\n        """Generate human-readable rationale for decision"""\n        \n        phase_str = f" in {phase.value} phase" if phase else ""\n        \n        if action == GateAction.PROCEED_AUTOMATICALLY:\n            return (\n                f"Confidence {confidence:.2f} significantly exceeds threshold {threshold:.2f}"\n                f"{phase_str} (margin: +{margin:.2f}). "\n                f"Proceeding automatically with high confidence."\n            )\n        \n        elif action == GateAction.PROCEED_WITH_MONITORING:\n            return (\n                f"Confidence {confidence:.2f} exceeds threshold {threshold:.2f}"\n                f"{phase_str} (margin: +{margin:.2f}). "\n                f"Proceeding with monitoring to track outcomes."\n            )\n        \n        elif action == GateAction.PROCEED_WITH_CAUTION:\n            return (\n                f"Confidence {confidence:.2f} meets threshold {threshold:.2f}"\n                f"{phase_str} (margin: {margin:+.2f}). "\n                f"Proceeding with caution - close monitoring recommended."\n            )\n        \n        elif action == GateAction.REQUEST_HUMAN_REVIEW:\n            return (\n                f"Confidence {confidence:.2f} slightly below threshold {threshold:.2f}"\n                f"{phase_str} (margin: {margin:+.2f}). "\n                f"Requesting human review before proceeding."\n            )\n        \n        elif action == GateAction.REQUIRE_HUMAN_APPROVAL:\n            return (\n                f"Confidence {confidence:.2f} below threshold {threshold:.2f}"\n                f"{phase_str} (margin: {margin:+.2f}). "\n                f"Requiring explicit human approval to proceed."\n            )\n        \n        else:  # BLOCK_EXECUTION\n            return (\n                f"Confidence {confidence:.2f} significantly below threshold {threshold:.2f}"\n                f"{phase_str} (margin: {margin:+.2f}). "\n                f"Execution blocked - confidence too low to proceed safely."\n            )\n    \n    def _log_decision(self, result: GateResult):\n        """Log gate decision"""\n        if result.allowed:\n            log_level = logging.INFO\n            status = "ALLOWED"\n        else:\n            log_level = logging.WARNING\n            status = "BLOCKED"\n        \n        logger.log(\n            log_level,\n            f"Murphy Gate {status}: confidence={result.confidence:.2f}, "\n            f"threshold={result.threshold:.2f}, margin={result.margin:+.2f}, "\n            f"action={result.action.value}"\n        )\n    \n    def set_phase_threshold(self, phase: Phase, threshold: float):\n        """Set custom threshold for a phase"""\n        if not 0.0 <= threshold <= 1.0:\n            raise ValueError("Threshold must be between 0.0 and 1.0")\n        \n        self.phase_thresholds[phase] = threshold\n        logger.info(f"Set {phase.value} phase threshold to {threshold:.2f}")\n    \n    def get_phase_threshold(self, phase: Phase) -> float:\n        """Get threshold for a phase"""\n        return self.phase_thresholds.get(phase, self.default_threshold)\n    \n    def get_all_thresholds(self) -> dict:\n        """Get all phase thresholds"""\n        return {\n            \'default\': self.default_threshold,\n            \'phases\': {phase.value: threshold for phase, threshold in self.phase_thresholds.items()}\n        }\n</create-file>\n</function_calls>'}

Weights for uncertainty-based confidence calculation\n        self.uncertainty_weights = {\n            \'data\': 0.25,\n            \'authority\': 0.20,\n            \'intent\': 0.15,\n            \'risk\': 0.25,\n            \'disagreement\': 0.15\n        }\n    \n    def validate(\n        self,\n        task: Any,\n        context: Dict[str, Any],\n        phase: Optional[Phase] = None,\n        threshold: Optional[float] = None\n    ) -> ConfidenceReport:\n        """\n        Complete validation of a task\n        \n        Args:\n            task: Task to validate\n            context: Execution context\n            phase: Current execution phase (optional)\n            threshold: Custom confidence threshold (optional)\n            \n        Returns:\n            ConfidenceReport with complete assessment\n        """\n        logger.info(f"Validating task: {getattr(task, \'task_id\', \'unknown\')}")\n        \n        # Compute uncertainty scores\n        uncertainty_scores = self.uncertainty_calculator.compute_all_uncertainties(\n            task=task,\n            context=context\n        )\n        \n        # Compute confidence from uncertainties\n        confidence = self._compute_confidence_from_uncertainties(uncertainty_scores)\n        \n        # Compute confidence using existing formula (if available)\n        confidence_v1 = None\n        if self.has_v1_calculator:\n            try:\n                confidence_v1 = self._compute_confidence_v1(task, context)\n            except Exception as e:\n                logger.warning(f"Could not compute v1 confidence: {e}")\n        \n        # Use higher confidence (conservative approach)\n        final_confidence = max(confidence, confidence_v1) if confidence_v1 else confidence\n        \n        # Evaluate Murphy Gate\n        gate_result = self.murphy_gate.evaluate(\n            confidence=final_confidence,\n            threshold=threshold,\n            phase=phase,\n            context=context\n        )\n        \n        # Generate detailed factors\n        factors = self._generate_factors(task, context, uncertainty_scores)\n        \n        # Generate recommendations\n        recommendations = self._generate_recommendations(\n            uncertainty_scores,\n            confidence,\n            gate_result\n        )\n        \n        # Generate warnings\n        warnings = self._generate_warnings(\n            uncertainty_scores,\n            confidence,\n            gate_result\n        )\n        \n        # Create report\n        report = ConfidenceReport(\n            uncertainty_scores=uncertainty_scores,\n            confidence=confidence,\n            confidence_v1=confidence_v1,\n            gate_result=gate_result,\n            factors=factors,\n            recommendations=recommendations,\n            warnings=warnings\n        )\n        \n        logger.info(\n            f"Validation complete: confidence={final_confidence:.2f}, "\n            f"gate_action={gate_result.action.value}"\n        )\n        \n        return report\n    \n    def _compute_confidence_from_uncertainties(\n        self,\n        uncertainty_scores: UncertaintyScores\n    ) -> float:\n        """\n        Compute confidence from uncertainty scores\n        \n        Formula: C = 1 - (w_d·UD + w_a·UA + w_i·UI + w_r·UR + w_g·UG)\n        \n        Where weights sum to 1.0\n        """\n        total_uncertainty = (\n            self.uncertainty_weights[\'data\'] * uncertainty_scores.UD +\n            self.uncertainty_weights[\'authority\'] * uncertainty_scores.UA +\n            self.uncertainty_weights[\'intent\'] * uncertainty_scores.UI +\n            self.uncertainty_weights[\'risk\'] * uncertainty_scores.UR +\n            self.uncertainty_weights[\'disagreement\'] * uncertainty_scores.UG\n        )\n        \n        confidence = 1.0 - total_uncertainty\n        \n        # Ensure in valid range\n        confidence = max(0.0, min(1.0, confidence))\n        \n        logger.debug(\n            f"Confidence from uncertainties: {confidence:.3f} "\n            f"(UD={uncertainty_scores.UD:.2f}, UA={uncertainty_scores.UA:.2f}, "\n            f"UI={uncertainty_scores.UI:.2f}, UR={uncertainty_scores.UR:.2f}, "\n            f"UG={uncertainty_scores.UG:.2f})"\n        )\n        \n        return confidence\n    \n    def _compute_confidence_v1(\n        self,\n        task: Any,\n        context: Dict[str, Any]\n    ) -> float:\n        """\n        Compute confidence using existing G/D/H formula\n        \n        This provides a comparison point and fallback.\n        """\n        if not self.has_v1_calculator:\n            return None\n        \n        # TODO: Integrate with actual confidence calculator\n        # For now, return a placeholder\n        return 0.75\n    \n    def _generate_factors(\n        self,\n        task: Any,\n        context: Dict[str, Any],\n        uncertainty_scores: UncertaintyScores\n    ) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        """Generate detailed factors contributing to scores"""\n        return {\n            \'data_quality\': self._categorize_score(1.0 - uncertainty_scores.UD),\n            \'source_credibility\': self._categorize_score(1.0 - uncertainty_scores.UA),\n            \'goal_clarity\': self._categorize_score(1.0 - uncertainty_scores.UI),\n            \'risk_level\': self._categorize_score(1.0 - uncertainty_scores.UR),\n            \'consensus_level\': self._categorize_score(1.0 - uncertainty_scores.UG),\n            \'task_priority\': getattr(task, \'priority\', \'unknown\'),\n            \'has_validation_criteria\': bool(getattr(task, \'validation_criteria\', [])),\n            \'has_human_checkpoints\': bool(getattr(task, \'human_checkpoints\', []))\n        }\n    \n    def _categorize_score(self, score: float) -> str:\n        """Categorize a score into quality levels"""\n        if score >= 0.9:\n            return \'excellent\'\n        elif score >= 0.7:\n            return \'good\'\n        elif score >= 0.5:\n            return \'fair\'\n        elif score >= 0.3:\n            return \'poor\'\n        else:\n            return \'very_poor\'\n    \n    def _generate_recommendations(\n        self,\n        uncertainty_scores: UncertaintyScores,\n        confidence: float,\n        gate_result: GateResult\n    ) -> list:\n        """Generate recommendations for improving confidence"""\n        recommendations = []\n        \n        # Data uncertainty recommendations\n        if uncertainty_scores.UD > 0.3:\n            recommendations.append(\n                "Consider additional data validation and verification to reduce data uncertainty"\n            )\n        \n        # Authority uncertainty recommendations\n        if uncertainty_scores.UA > 0.3:\n            recommendations.append(\n                "Verify source credentials and seek expert consensus to reduce authority uncertainty"\n            )\n        \n        # Intent uncertainty recommendations\n        if uncertainty_scores.UI > 0.3:\n            recommendations.append(\n                "Clarify requirements and add measurable success criteria to reduce intent uncertainty"\n            )\n        \n        # Risk uncertainty recommendations\n        if uncertainty_scores.UR > 0.3:\n            recommendations.append(\n                "Implement risk mitigation strategies and increase reversibility to reduce risk uncertainty"\n            )\n        \n        # Disagreement uncertainty recommendations\n        if uncertainty_scores.UG > 0.3:\n            recommendations.append(\n                "Resolve conflicting information and establish decision authority to reduce disagreement uncertainty"\n            )\n        \n        # Gate-specific recommendations\n        if not gate_result.allowed:\n            recommendations.append(\n                f"Confidence {confidence:.2f} is below threshold {gate_result.threshold:.2f}. "\n                f"Address the above recommendations before proceeding."\n            )\n        \n        return recommendations\n    \n    def _generate_warnings(\n        self,\n        uncertainty_scores: UncertaintyScores,\n        confidence: float,\n        gate_result: GateResult\n    ) -> list:\n        """Generate warnings about potential issues"""\n        warnings = []\n        \n        # High uncertainty warnings\n        if uncertainty_scores.UD > 0.7:\n            warnings.append("WARNING: Very high data uncertainty - data quality is poor")\n        \n        if uncertainty_scores.UA > 0.7:\n            warnings.append("WARNING: Very high authority uncertainty - source credibility is questionable")\n        \n        if uncertainty_scores.UI > 0.7:\n            warnings.append("WARNING: Very high intent uncertainty - requirements are unclear")\n        \n        if uncertainty_scores.UR > 0.7:\n            warnings.append("WARNING: Very high risk uncertainty - potential for significant negative consequences")\n        \n        if uncertainty_scores.UG > 0.7:\n            warnings.append("WARNING: Very high disagreement uncertainty - major conflicts in information")\n        \n        # Low confidence warnings\n        if confidence < 0.5:\n            warnings.append("WARNING: Confidence is very low - execution is not recommended")\n        \n        # Gate warnings\n        if gate_result.action == \'block_execution\':\n            warnings.append("CRITICAL: Murphy Gate has blocked execution - do not proceed")\n        \n        return warnings\n    \n    def get_uncertainty_breakdown(\n        self,\n        task: Any,\n        context: Dict[str, Any]\n    ) -> Dict[str, float]:\n        """Get detailed uncertainty breakdown"""\n        uncertainty_scores = self.uncertainty_calculator.compute_all_uncertainties(\n            task=task,\n            context=context\n        )\n        \n        return uncertainty_scores.to_dict()\n    \n    def evaluate_gate_only(\n        self,\n        confidence: float,\n        phase: Optional[Phase] = None,\n        threshold: Optional[float] = None\n    ) -> GateResult:\n        """Evaluate Murphy Gate without full validation"""\n        return self.murphy_gate.evaluate(\n            confidence=confidence,\n            threshold=threshold,\n            phase=phase\n        )\n</create-file>\n</function_calls>'}

{'role': 'assistant', 'content': '<function_calls>\n<create-file file_path="murphy_implementation/execution/context.py">\n"""\nExecution Context\n\nMaintains state and context throughout task execution.\n"""\n\nfrom typing import Dict, Any, List, Optional\nfrom datetime import datetime\nfrom dataclasses import dataclass, field\n\n\n@dataclass\nclass ExecutionContext:\n    """\n    Execution context that maintains state throughout task execution\n    \n    This context is passed through all phases and accumulates:\n    - Phase outputs\n    - Assumptions\n    - Validation results\n    - Human interventions\n    - Audit trail\n    """\n    \n    # Task information\n    task_id: str\n    task: Any\n    execution_mode: str = "supervised"\n    confidence_threshold: float = 0.7\n    \n    # Current state\n    current_phase: Optional[str] = None\n    phase_completed: bool = False\n    \n    # Accumulated outputs\n    phase_outputs: Dict[str, Any] = field(default_factory=dict)\n    final_output: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None\n    \n    # Confidence tracking\n    confidence: float = 0.0\n    confidence_history: List[Dict[str, float]] = field(default_factory=list)\n    \n    # Risk tracking\n    risk_score: float = 0.0\n    risk_history: List[Dict[str, float]] = field(default_factory=list)\n    \n    # Assumptions\n    assumptions: List[str] = field(default_factory=list)\n    invalidated_assumptions: List[str] = field(default_factory=list)\n    \n    # Human interaction\n    human_approved: bool = False\n    human_interventions: List[Dict[str, Any]] = field(default_factory=list)\n    \n    # Audit trail\n    audit_trail: List[Dict[str, Any]] = field(default_factory=list)\n    \n    # Metadata\n    started_at: datetime = field(default_factory=datetime.now)\n    metadata: Dict[str, Any] = field(default_factory=dict)\n    \n    def update(self, phase_result: Dict[str, Any]):\n        """Update context with phase result"""\n        phase = phase_result.get(\'phase\')\n        \n        if phase:\n            self.phase_outputs[phase] = phase_result.get(\'output\', {})\n            self.current_phase = phase\n            self.phase_completed = True\n            \n            # Update confidence\n            if \'confidence\' in phase_result:\n                self.confidence = phase_result[\'confidence\']\n                self.confidence_history.append({\n                    \'phase\': phase,\n                    \'confidence\': phase_result[\'confidence\'],\n                    \'timestamp\': datetime.now().isoformat()\n                })\n            \n            # Update risk\n            if \'risk_score\' in phase_result:\n                self.risk_score = phase_result[\'risk_score\']\n                self.risk_history.append({\n                    \'phase\': phase,\n                    \'risk_score\': phase_result[\'risk_score\'],\n                    \'timestamp\': datetime.now().isoformat()\n                })\n            \n            # Add to audit trail\n            self.audit_trail.append({\n                \'event\': \'phase_completed\',\n                \'phase\': phase,\n                \'timestamp\': datetime.now().isoformat(),\n                \'confidence\': self.confidence,\n                \'risk_score\': self.risk_score\n            })\n    \n    def add_assumption(self, assumption: str):\n        """Add an assumption"""\n        if assumption not in self.assumptions:\n            self.assumptions.append(assumption)\n            self.audit_trail.append({\n                \'event\': \'assumption_added\',\n                \'assumption\': assumption,\n                \'timestamp\': datetime.now().isoformat()\n            })\n    \n    def invalidate_assumption(self, assumption: str, reason: str):\n        """Invalidate an assumption"""\n        if assumption in self.assumptions and assumption not in self.invalidated_assumptions:\n            self.invalidated_assumptions.append(assumption)\n            self.audit_trail.append({\n                \'event\': \'assumption_invalidated\',\n                \'assumption\': assumption,\n                \'reason\': reason,\n                \'timestamp\': datetime.now().isoformat()\n            })\n    \n    def add_human_intervention(self, intervention_type: str, details: Dict[str, Any]):\n        """Record human intervention"""\n        intervention = {\n            \'type\': intervention_type,\n            \'details\': details,\n            \'timestamp\': datetime.now().isoformat()\n        }\n        self.human_interventions.append(intervention)\n        self.audit_trail.append({\n            \'event\': \'human_intervention\',\n            \'intervention\': intervention,\n            \'timestamp\': datetime.now().isoformat()\n        })\n    \n    def log_event(self, event_type: str, details: Dict[str, Any]):\n        """Log an event to audit trail"""\n        self.audit_trail.append({\n            \'event\': event_type,\n            \'details\': details,\n            \'timestamp\': datetime.now().isoformat()\n        })\n    \n    def get_phase_output(self, phase: str) -> Optional[Dict[str, Any]]:\n        """Get output from a specific phase"""\n        return self.phase_outputs.get(phase)\n    \n    def has_invalidated_assumptions(self) -> bool:\n        """Check if any assumptions have been invalidated"""\n        return len(self.invalidated_assumptions) > 0\n    \n    def get_confidence_trend(self) -> str:\n        """Get confidence trend (improving/stable/declining)"""\n        if len(self.confidence_history) < 2:\n            return "stable"\n        \n        recent = [h[\'confidence\'] for h in self.confidence_history[-3:]]\n        \n        if all(recent[i] < recent[i+1] for i in range(len(recent)-1)):\n            return "improving"\n        elif all(recent[i] > recent[i+1] for i in
